0 The Apostles' Creed

Anon.
Doh is G

Pa Pathian Bangkim hihthei,
Lei leh Van siam ka ging;
Huan, A Tapa tang neihsun Jesu Khrist,
I Toupa leng ka ging.

Amah Khasiangthou paisakin,
Mari sung hong suak hi;
Pontia Pilat nuai ah thuaka,
Krosa kilhden a om.

A sih zoh chianga,
Hankhuka vuia om;
Nuailam misi khuaa vahoh a,
Ni thum ni a thounawn.

Vana kahtou nawnta,
Pathian taklama tu;
Mihing leh misi vaihawm dingin,
Van pan hong pai nawn ding.

Khasiangthou ka ginga,
Saptuam siangthou khat;
Misiang kigawmna zong,
Khelhnate ngaihdamna, pumpi thohnawnna,
Tangtawn hinna ka ging. Amen.

C3 Phat Ding Na Kilawm Hi

Key G

Phat ding Na kilawm hi Toupa Jesu,
Pahtawi ding Na kilawm hi;
Phat ding Na kilawm hi Toupa,
Minthanna khempeuh ngah ding;

    Vangletna khempeuh,
    Uk zohna khempeuh,
    A tawntung phat ding in Na kilawm hi,
    Vangletna khempeuh
    Uk zohna khempeuh,
    A tawntung phat ding in Na kilawm hi.

C2 Toupa Hong Bia Ing

Key G

Hongzuan ing Nang kia hong bia ding in,
Hongzuan ing vangletna pia di'n

    Toupa hong bia ing,
    Nang hong bia ing,

    Nang hong bia ing,
    Na min siangthou siangthou hi.

C4 Sam No. 5

Doh is G

Kong kipumpiak hong sang in;
Limtak in hong ngaihkhiak in ka kah aw,
Ka Kumpipa ka Pathian,
Nang kiang hongthum ka hi ngal a,
Jing tengin ka aw na za zel ding,
Toupa jingkhangin
Nang kiang kong thum ding a,
Nangmah kia hong mit suan ning.

C1 Lungsung Nuama Kidim Toh

Lungsung nuam leh kipahthu gen ni,
A siangthou Pa kiang,
Amah Tapa Jesu Khrist
Eite hong pia hi.

    Ahat lou in kei ka hat chi hen,
    A zawng in ka hau chi hen,
    Toupa'n ei dia hon hihsakte hang in,
    A hatlou in kei ka hat chi hen,
    A zawng in ka hau chi hen,
    Toupa'n ei dia hon hih sak-te hang in,
    Nuam ni.

1 Jesu Min Lian Phat Chiat Ni E

Edward Perronet
Doh is G

Jesu minlian phat chiat ni e,
Angelte'n bia'n kun hen;
Mangpen' lukhu honla unla,
Khusak un miteng' Lal!

Martarte'n Amah khusak un,
A maitam pan hong sam;
Phat un Jese Jikpi phat un,
Khusak un miteng' Lal!

Nou Israel chitelte aw,
Omsun hatlou leh tawm;
Na Hondampa uh phat unla,
Khusak un miteng' Lal!

Nou Jentel gilou te'n thei un,
A thuakna ngilh kei un;
Koih un gallu A khebul ah,
Khusak un miteng' Lal!

Namchih, pauchih, mi khempeuh te,
Hiai leitung-a teng te;
Lalna khempeuh Amah pia un,
Khusak un miteng' Lal!

Aw tungchiang mi pawl siangthou toh,
A khebul ah kun le'ng;
Tangtawn Amah phat la sa-in,
Khusak ni miteng' Lal!

@ Labu 2019

2 Pathian Hon Phat Ung

William P Mackay
Doh is G

Pathian, hon phat ung!
Na Ta it Jesu ziak'!
Amah si-in thounawn,
Tu'n van ah om hi.

    Haleluia, Nang na vanglian,
    Haleluia, Amen;
    Haleluia, Nang na vanglian,
    Hon halhsak nawn in.

Pathian, honphat ung!
Na Kha Siangthou ziakin;
Aman Hondampa honhilh,
Zan mial thengsak.

Phatna thupina,
Thahsa Belamnou'a;
Aman i khelhna pua,
I nitna siangsak.

Hon halhsak nawn in,
Na itna'n hon dimsak;
Michih' kha Na mei in,
Hon kuangsak nawn in.

@ Labu 2019

3 Aw Pathian Tanga Hong Panpih

Isaac Watts
Doh is C

Aw Pathian, tanga hon panpih,
Machiang ka lamet uh;
Huihpi vuahpi nuaia bitna,
Tangtawn-a ka inn uh.

Na mangtutphah limnuai belin,
Na misiangte bit uh;
Na khut in honpii honkai in,
Ka bit ding uh, Toupa.

Gammual tangbang kikhun ma in,
Leitung a om khiak ma'n;
Pathian hi chia tangtawn apan,
Tangtawn tulmawh Na hi.

Nang ding in kum sang tampi zong,
Mitphiat kal a ching lou;
Tuma, tunung, kou ka chih uh,
Nang, Tu, na chi gige.

Hunin chiautuipi luang bangin,
Mihingte taimang hi;
Zan a mang zingkal a bei bang,
Mihingte ngilhin om.

Aw Pathian, tanga hon panpih,
Machiang ka lamet uh;
Damsung teng honchingpa hi in.
Tangtawn-a ka inn uh.

@ Labu 2019

4 Theih Vuallouh In Pathian Gamtang

Doh is C

Theihvualouh-in Pathian gamtang,
A lamdang na sem ding';
Tuipi tung sik bangin paia,
Huihpi tung bang ah tuang.

Tehvuallouh thukpi lei nuaiah
Zia kilawm vante koih;
Amah deihbangin na sema,
Sem khial, bawl khial ngeilou.

Nou misiang, lauthawngte, hang un,
Meipi na lauh un zong '
Zahngaihna tampi tun nou ding'
Vualzawlna'n hongzu ding.

Theitawmin Toupa mawhsa ken,
A hehpihna muang jaw'n;
A maigum na muhte ah zong,
A nuihmai kisel hi.

A tupte buching pah ding hi,
Dakkal tengin nai hi;
Tuin haksa tadih mahleh,
Buchin nuam mahmah ding.

Ginlahna zaw khial mahmah ding,
Pathian' khutsuak haih ding;
Pathian kiain genchian theia,
A gingtami hilh ding.

5 Tangtawn La Kilawm Ngai Un

J L Sterling
Doh is G

Tangtawn la kilawm ngai un,
Vana hong kipan;
'Thupi Pathian thupi hen,
Tung Pathian,' chi,
Vakna munnuam akipan,
Angel leh misiangthou lasak,
Ngaihtak-a tum leh kikou;
'Toupa Mangpen.'

Vualzohna la ngai dih un,
Khovel tengteng thawn;
Tuipi luangging bangin ngaih,
Jaknop mahmah;
'Halleluia, Toupa hi,'
Vualzohna la gam tengteng ah,
Aw ngaih leh nakpi-a sa'n;
'Toupa Mangpen.'

Nuamsa Thumte phat chiat un,
Nou van mipite;
Phat un, Pa phat un, Tapa
Leh Kha Siangthou;
Tangtawna a hih bangin,
Tangtawn tangtawn in gingging hen,
Tatsate'n gengen ding uh,
'Toupa Mangpen.'

6 Kanan Juan I Pai

Paulina
Doh is F

Kanan juan i pai, puanlap khaia la sa'n,
Gilou doudinga kipia sepaih i hi;
Hizong galdou lai kikhen i om louhna'ng,
Toupa' lam pang kua kua chiin kidong hang.

    Aw i lak uah kua ahiam, thutak-a muanhuai,
    Thutak gum a ding ding, Toupa lama pang?
    Aw i lak uah kua ahiam, thutaka muanhuai,
    Thutak guma ding ding, Toupa lama pang?

Temsau leh galvante te solsol thei hi,
Setan zong vak sawltak bang kibawl thei hi;
Hizong lungtang ah muanhuailouhna om thei,
'Toupa lam pang ka hi,' kam in a chih hang'.

I lak uah kuahiam vaihawmna nuai a om,
Pathian zahngaihna ngaihdamna neilou lai;
Lungtang kisathei niamkhiak in honla in,
Toupa'n hon ngak laiin Amah lam juan meng'.

Dahna, natna leh bawlsiatna khawksa ken,
I thuma khawisatna la suak pah ding hi;
I zuih muanhuai ei hon Pipa Khros pua in,
Vualzou i kikou ding; Toupa' lam' pang hang.

@ Labu 2019

7 Khasiang Ka Sung Hong Teng Den In

E H Stokes
Doh is C

Kha Siang, ka sung' hong tengden in,
Ka lungtang ling hong sil in;
Siangthouna-in kei hong luah in,
Hong pai-in, hong dimsak in.

    Hong dimsak', hong dimsak',
    Jesu aw, tu'n hong dimsak';
    Siangthouna in kei hong luah in,
    Hong pai-in hong dimsak in.

Hon hehpih Kha, non dimsak thei,
Dim dan kon hilh theih louh hang;
Ka taksap tawntung Nang na hi,
Hong pai-in, hong dimsak in.

Kei a jawngkhal tawntung hi'ng e,
Na maiah tu'n hong kun ing;
Tangtawn Pathian Kha nuamsa aw,
Na tha tawh hong dimsak in.

Hongsil, hong khamuan, hong hong in,
Siangsak in hong vualjawl in;
Nong khamuan ding nong hongkhia ding,
Nong dimsak ding hi, tuin.

8 Aw Toupa, Tungnung Pen

Upa Thanga
Doh is Bb

Aw Toupa tungnungpen, lambang hon pak ung,
Pathian hing leh bangkim hihthei Nang na hi;
Nuaisiahte, tengkhawi, liangvai, giloute' Lawm,
Sanggah, gentheite teng' Toupa leh Pathian.

Thumnate dawngpa Pathian na hih jiakin,
Na mite'n taksap hon nget uh Na pe jel;
Na tate' kah leh mau Nang na ngaikhe jel,
Thudik gum, na hoih sem, Na pampaih kei hi.

Na thu hoih mijawng leh haute zasak in,
Midang Nang hon doute'n zong zata uhen;
Tu-a hotdama ka om samna ding un,
Bang a hiam ka hih ding, chi uh hen, Amen.

Namchih mial paisan, leh sal suak kipak hen,
Tungnungpen ah Pathian thupipen hen aw;
A kipahpih leimite lak' lem leng hen,
Hosana, Hosana, chi-in sa uh hen.

Huan, namchih kiang ah Na min zahtak huai hen,
Na gam thupitak-in hong tung jel hen aw;
Van- a mi'n a hih bang-un leia mite'n,
Na deihlam hih henla, gam chih ah, Amen.

@ Labu 2019

9 Aw Hotdamna Ja Aw Itna

William Boots
Kaih No.8

Aw hotdamna ja! aw itna tuipi thuk,
Zahngaihna lian, Khrist-in tunglam pan hontun;
Khovel pum tatna manpha athawna piak,
Miteng dia tua luangin, kei zong hontum in!

Ka khelhna a tam, ka nitnate a thuk,
Khelh lungkham ka kahna khitui luang a tam;
Ka kah phatuam lou, sisan tuipi luangin -
Tun non silsiang thei hi, kei zong hontum in!

Ka lungtom, sinsiat leh utna giloute'n,
Ka kha henchipin honkhialsak hamtang hi;
Tuipi manpha luang ah suahtakna ka mu,
Thilhihthei hongluang in, kei zong hontum in!

Khemnaten honsualin, lauhnaten hondelh,
Lungnop, phattuamna beiin kum tam ka hing;
A hoihzaw ka tang ngei ding chih ka thei hi,
Khatvei hontum lechin, Na sianna tui in.

Aw zahngaihna tuipi, nang hinna pethei,
Tui lamdang, na piautak ah kong ding ngeita;
Siansakna tuipi tuin kong tung nawn hi,
Ka puma non tup ma'n, ka kik nawnlou ding.

Tu'n tuipi luang, ken a tui ka khoih kha hi,
Hondam dia Hat-in honsapna ka ja hi;
Ka ginna'n muang ngamta, hotdam hi ngei ding,
Damna tui ah ka bual, tuin hontum hi!

Halleluia! tu'n zaw ka damsung nite,
A phatna dingin phaltakin ka zang ding;
Aman A sapum liamin kitamsak hi,
Hotdamna tuipi ja, A luansak theihna'n.

@ Labu 2019

10 Pathian' Itna, Itna Tungnung

C Wesley
Doh is Bb

Pathian' itna, itna tungnung,
Van kipahna hong kum in;
Kou ah Na tenna hong bawl in,
Na hehpihna hong khusak';
Jesu, Nang mi Na hehpih thei,
Itna ngenin Na dim a;
Hotdamna in kou hong veh in,
Hon ngaite' siang ah lut in.

Na itna Laukha pia inla,
Mi lungkhamte' lungsung ah;
Bangteng Nang ah hong luahsak in,
Na chiam khawlna hon musak;
Khelh utna lamangta inla,
Alpha leh Omega hi'n;
Ginna bul leh a tawpna Nang,
Suahtakna hon pia ta in.

Hong pai in, Nang hondam dia hat,
Nangmah' hinna hon neisak;
Kou-a teng ding, hongkik pah in,
Na tempul nusia ngeike'n;
Nangmah kon phat gige ding uh,
Nangmah na sem gige in;
Nangmah phat-in kong thum ding ua,
Na itna kia suang gige'n.

Khaile, Na siamthak zou ngalin,
Siangthou leh deihhuai hi n'ung;
Ka hotdamna uh Nangmah ah,
Kimtaka om mu nuam ung;
Thupi semsem hong hita n'ung,
Vangam kong tun tanpha un;
Lamdang, itna, phatna-a dim,
Na mai'h bangkim ngak dongin.

@ Labu 2019

11 Kei Tanga Ding Pa Jesu Hi

Kei tang' zumna thuak laitak';

12 Kipak Sak Ding Jesu Hongpai

Mrs Frank A Breck
Doh is Eb

Kipaksak ding Jesu hongpai,
Itna tan chiang';
A lungkhamte lungnuamsak ding,
Itna tan chiang';
Itna'n thum dan hon hilh ding,
Lungkham dahna lamang ding,
Miallak khua vaksak ding hi,
Itna tan chiang'.

    Itna tan chiang',
    Itna tan chiang';
    Lungsung panin la kisathei,
    Itna tan chiang',
    Itna tan chiang',
    Itna tan chiang',
    Midangte lungnopna puak thei,
    Itna tan chiang'.

Leitung pumpi hong kilawm ding,
Itna tan chiang';
Nasep zong lungnopna hi ding,
Itna tan chiang';
Gim thuakna zong siangthou ding,
Lungsung muanna omden ding,
Nuntakna manpha tuam ding,
Itna tan chiang'.

Dah lungkhamna hong nuamtuam ding,
Itna tan chiang';
Lungsung puakgik hong jang tuam ding,
Itna tan chiang';
Vangletna hong tang ding a,
Paina'ng lampi honhilh ding,
Lungsung nopna ki-ngah ding,
Itna tan chiang'.

Tullou thupina ngahta ni,
Itna tan chiang';
Lawmte itna taktak piang ding,
Itna tan chiang';
Leitung vualzohna ngah chiang',
Vantung nuntak kipat chiang',
Nisa vak kul nawnlou ding,
Itna tangta.

13 Itna Lamdang

John Newton
Doh is G

Itna lamdang! A min ngaih e,
Kei bang kihhuai hon hut;
Kei ka mangkhin tu'n A hon mu,
Mitdel tu'n ka mu thei.

Tua itna'n laudan hon sinsak,
Itna'n ka lau beisak;
Tua itna manpha lawmlawm e,
Ka gintak laitak in.

Lauhuai gimna, thang tampi lak',
Kei ka paisuakta hi;
Itna kia hi tutan hon pii,
Itna'n inn hon tun ding.

Ka pumpi leh lungsim bah a,
Ka lei hinna bei chiang;
Tua puanjak sungah ken ngah ning,
Hinna nuam leh muanna.

Tua munnuama ni bang tanga,
Kum sangsawm i vei chiang';
Pathian phat la kiam lou lai ding,
Phatna ni kiam lou ding.

@ Labu 2019

14 Pathian Chitna Lamdangpen

Lyman G Cuyler
Doh is D

Pathian chitna lamdangpen pen la in sa ni,
A hon khotuah leh ven gige na;
I kipumpiakna gimnamtui bang zaam tou hen,
Thuum a Amai a i kihop chiang.

    Amah phat in bia ni, A silbawl te vang in,
    A hoihna leh khotuahna gen ni;
    I kipumpiakna gimnamtui bang zaam tou hen,
    Thuum a Amai a i kihop chiang.

A hehpihna thilpiak lamdang la in sa ni,
Itna in tua teng a hon musak;
A tapa Jesu toh i kikholhna nuam ah,
Tua in A mangtutphah hon naihsak.

A vualzawlna in hon zui zel ding in thum ni,
I lampi A hon vaksak na di'n;
Ei Amah a i hong buchin theihna ding in,
A vangam thupi i luahna ding.

16 Ka Mit In Toupa Thupi

Julia Wark Howe
Doh is C

Ka mit in Toupa thupi-a hongpailai
A na muta,
A lunghehna grepkhuk a kipan in
A chilkhe lel hi!
A namsau hiamtak leh lauhuaitak leh kin
A phawikheta,
I Pathian a kuankhia.

    Thupi, thupi, Haleluiah,
    Thupi, thupi, Haleluiah,
    Thupi, thupi, Haleluiah,
    I Pathian a kuankhia

Puan um zakhat venna mei tampi lak ah
A mel honglang,
Amah din nitak dai kiak hun leh vot ah
Maitam bawl uh;
A vaihawmna thu meivak kuangtak leh vak ah
Ka sim thei,
I Pathian a kuankhia.

Nungkik ngeilou ding-a sepna dingin pengkul
A hong ging,
Aw, vaihawmna mangtutphah ma-a mite
Lung ommoh sak;
Aw, ka kha kinin, Amah panpi'n ka kha
Kipak om in,
I Pathian a kuankhia.

Lili pallun lai in Khrist hong piang lei-a
Mite' kiang ah,
Nang leh kei hon hih lamdang thei, loupina
Hon pianpih a;
Mihingte' siangthouna din a si, suahtak
Na'n si ngap leng,
I Pathian kuankhiak lai.

17 Immanuel Nak Liam Apan

W Cowper
Doh is C

Immanuel nakliam apan,
Sisan lui hong luang khia;
Tua sisan lui migilou ding',
Gitlouh silsiangna hi.

Gilou si ding a kilh un zong,
Tua lui mu man-in nuam;
Amah bangin gilou leng zong,
Tua ah ka siang ding hi.

Ka it Belamnou, Na si pha'n,
Thahat mansuah ngei lou;
Tatsa saptuam khial nawn lou dia,
Hotkhiak a hih dong in.

Na liamma pan sisan lui luang,
Muanna toh ka muh nung;
Tatna itna hi ka thupi
Ka sih mateng gen ning.

Kei dangawk pi hankhuk sunga
Dai dide' ka jal chiang,
Tuachiang' la ngaihjaw'n honphat ning,
Hondam dia Na hatna.

18 Pathian I Kulhpi Muanhuai Hi

Martin Luther
Doh is D

Pathian i Kulhpi muanhuai hi,
A kip tawntung Kulhpi hi;
Amah eite hon huhpa hi,
Gitlouh tuipi tung' vualzou;
Tanglai pan melmapa'n,
Siatna ngenta a zong;
A pilna leh hatna,
Huatna ngen in a dim;
A kimpih leitung om lou.

Eimah hatna in dou lehang,
I zou ngeikei hial ding hi;
Mitakpa panpih louh in jaw,
Amah Pathian' Mitelpa;
Amah kua ahi hiam?
Amah Khrist Jesu hi!
Toupa Sabath A min,
Kikheng thei ngeilou hi;
Aman kidouna zou ding.

Leitung dawi ngenin dim henla,
Honhihsiat tum mahle uh '
Lau kei ni; Pathian-in deihzou,
Ei-a A Thutak vualzoh.
Neihlehlam teng mang hen,
It teng, lei hinna zong;
Pumpi zong that uhen;
Pathian' Thutak omden,
A gam tangtawnin omden.

19 Jesu A Lawm Hoih I Neih Dan

J Scriven
Doh is F

Jesu a Lawmhoih i neih dan,
I gitlouh dahna po ding;
Hamphathuai mahmah i hilh theih,
Bangteng Pathian kiang thumna'n;
Aw, lungmuanna tam i na tan,
Aw, nat thuak louh ding i thuak;
Amah i hilh louh vang hi e,
Bangteng Pathian kiang' thumna'n.

Ze-et leh khem-in i om hiam,
Buaina koipeuh a om hiam?
Lunglel ngeilou-in om ni e,
Bangteng Toupa' kiang thumna'n;
Tuabang Lawm muanhuai i mu diam,
I lungkham hon thuakpih ding;
I hatlouhna Jesun thei vek,
Bangteng Toupa kiang' thumna'n.

Hatlou leh gik pua'n i om hiam,
Damsung khosak ngaihtuahna'n?
Hondampa Hoih i bitna hi,
Bangteng Toupa kiang' thumna'n;
Simmoh leh ngilh-in na om hiam?
Toupa kiang thumna'n gen in;
A angsung ah a hon pom ding,
Lungmuanna tua'h na mu ding.

@ Labu 2019

20 Ginna'n Hon En Tou Ing

Ray Palmer
Doh is Eb

Ginna'n hon entou ing,
Kalvari Belamnou,
Ka Hondampa;
Ka thumna ngaikhia in,
Ka mohna honthuk ken;
Aw tuni'n ka pum in
Hon siangsak in.

Ka laukha sawlsapna,
Hehpihna'n hatsak in,
Aw, Pa Pathian;
Ka tang Na hong sita,
Ken leng hon it thei ta'ng;
Aw kon itna dai thei-
Kei leh chi veng.

Leitung buaina miallak,
Heina ka vaih lai in,
Hon pi jel in;
Ka ma mial vaksak in,
Lungkhamna thengsak in;
Mang ding hon phal nawn ke'n
Aw Pa Pathian.

Hinna pak vulna dia,
Sihna lui mial kon kan
Dektak chiang in;
Toupa, hon hehpih in,
Ka ban hon na kai in;
Tatsa gamlei thangvan
Hon kaipih in.

Ka dahna teng zong pua. (2)

Ka kipahna teng zong;
Sihna tunga zohna honpia,
Hankhuk pan hon hondam. (2)

A tenna van munnuam lam ah,
Ka khe tawl A tonpih;
Ka Pathian' thupina hon lak,
Ka dahna tengteng zong pua. (2)

A hauhdan bangjelin hon pia,

Toupa, Nang kon pia ding. (2)

Tungnungpen ah thupi hen chi'n la sa ning,
Pathian thuchiamte ah ka ding hi.

    Ding in, ding in,
    Pathian ka Hondampa thuchiamte a ding in,
    Ding in, ding in,
    Ka Pathian thuchiamte ah ka ding hi.

A juauthei ngeilou thuchiamte a ding in,
Ginlahna leh launa huih in honmut chiang;
Pathian thu hing zangin kei ka vualzou ding,
Pathian thuchiamte ah ka ding hi.

Thuchiamte a ding in tu'n ken ka mu thei,
Sianna sisan hoih kim kei ding a tua om;
Khrist in a bawl tua suahtakna siksan in,
Pathian thuchiamte ah ka ding hi.

Khrist keimah Toupa thuchiamte a ding in,
Itna khau in Amah toh kei honkan den;
Kha namsau zanga nisima vualzou-in,
Pathian thuchiamte ah ka ding hi.

Thuchiamte a ding kei ka puk theikei ding,
Mitphiatkal tenga Kha sapna aw ngaiin;
Ka bangkima bangkim, Honpa a khawlin,
Pathian thuchiamte ah ka ding hi.

Tanglai Lumsuang kei dia khi'n,

112 Khrist Leh Saptuam Di'n

E E Hewit
Doh is D

'Khrist leh Saptuam di'n i aw suah ni,
Eite Kumpipa nuamsa min ngaih pahtawi ve ni;
Tuailai thahatna-in kilawp-in sem ni,
Thutak gam adi'n muanhuai takin ding ni.

    Hon Tanpa Khrist deihhuai di'n,
    Hondam dia si Khrist di'n;
    Sisana A lei Saptuam di'n,
    Siangsak', hangsak', Toupa.

'Khrist leh Saptuam di'n' nakpi'n thum ni,
Niteng khros pua-in eite'n A puanlap jui ve ni;
Kipia ni, i pum-in, Kha thahatna ah;
Hun hoih pen ah muanhuai-in A na sem ni.

'Khrist leh Saptuam di'n' it lou pia ni,
Hun leh talent leh sum-le-pai Heutupa adi'n;

I puk jel hangin ginna'n i vualzou ding;
Amah i Honpa'n i hatna thaksak ding,
Jesu lam en gige'n, honpii tawntung ding.

Lei ah i Honpa hongtengta.

Zahdan siam, thumandan siam;
Nu kingainiam it-in enjui,
A ban kham-in A lum hi;
Khristian naupangte tengteng leng,
Amah bang thumang ding ahi.

Amah naupangte Etjui di'n,
Niteng ei bangin A khang;
Amah hatlou, panpihbei hi,
Ei bang' dah leh nuam theita;
Ei' lungkhamna hongthuakpih hi,
I nuamna zong hontanpih hi.

Hun tawp chiang'Amah i mu ding,
A hongtatna itna hang;
Tua naupang deihhuai leh nunnem,
Aman A tate pii jel hi,
Amah a paina munmun ah.

Tua gan-inn sung ah hilouin,
Bawngte omna hilouin;
Amah i mu ding vantung ah;
Pathian taklam ah tu hi,
Aksi bang lukhu khuk chiangin,
Puan ngou silh taten um ding hi.

    Tua chiang' ka kha'n Honpa Pathian honphat,

    Hotdam dingin,
    Ba' tua omlou ding?

Jingchiang khua hongvak ngeilou thei,
Na maimit zulhjau vualzawl di'n;
Tu a hun hi, mawk om nawn ken,
Tu'n hotdam' om in.

I Toupa'n hehpi'n hon ngakngak,
Hon itna it thuk lou ding maw?
Nang deihlam tawpsan ngal mai ve,
Tu'n hotdam' om in.

I Toupa'n kuamah nial neilou,
A hinna tang nuam laukhate;
Ging in, jui' nasep zawhsa hi,
Tu'n hotdam' om in.

271 A Sangzaw Lam Ka Delh Tawntung

Rev Hohnson Oatman, Jr.
Doh is Ab

A sangzaw lam ka delh tawntung,
A sangzaw mun nisim ka tung,
Ka paikawm in ka thum tawntung,
Toupa, a sangzaw mun' honpi'n.

    Toupa, hondingsak in ginna'n,
    A sanna mun vanmun khawng ah;
    Ka tunkhitna sanga sangzaw,
    Toupa, a sangzaw mun' honpi'n.

Toupa omden ka ut kei hi;
Tua bang mun ah midang om zong,
Ken zaw mun sangzaw ka tum hi.

Setan thalte'n honkap zongleh;
Ginna'n pahna la zata hi,
Mun sangzawa misiangte la.

A sanna mun tak kah ka nuam,
Thupina vak muh ka nuam hi;
Van ka tun matan ka thum ding,
Toupa, a sangzaw mun' honpi'n.

Khua vakden-a jan om nawn ngeilouh chiang',
Thupina tangtawn ni a tanden chiang',
Ka lungkim ding, lungkim mahmahta ding!

    Ka lungkimta ding hi,
    Ka lungkimta ding hi;
    Tua jingsang kilawma ka khanlawh chiang'. D.S.

Na thupina maituaha ka muh chiang',
Na tate Na angsung-a Na pom chiang';
Na hehpihna hauh Non etsak vek chiang',
Ka lungkim ding, lungkim mahmahta ding.

Ka it leh ngaih teng ka muh hun chiangin,
Sawta khensa ka itte ka pom chiang';
Kei dia Na muanhuai dan teng ka muh chiang',
Ka lungkim ding, lungkim mahmahta ding.

Kei dinga hinna Pepa ka muh chiang',
Mit vaktaka A mel ka etchian chiang';
Tangtawn la ngaiha Amah ka phat chiang',
Ka lungkim ding, lungkim mahmahta ding.

317 Tanna, Dahna Leh Mialna Apan

Jesu, Na kiang kon zuan.

Na deih leh kipah lama om di'n,
Jesu, Na kiang kon zuan,

Na itna nuama teng di'n kon zuan;
Tung lama vakhu bang a lengin,
Jesu, Na kiang kon zuan.

Tui thukna mun ah tummang pah ding uhi.

Mangthang den ding, tummang pah tading uh;
Kinmeng in, sanggam aw, zekai nawn ken,
Tuni'n Hinna-Khau khak', amau hondam in.

    Tangthu kumlui honhilh in.
    Jesu leh A itna.

Tangthu kumlui honhilh in,
Ka theih theihna ding in;
Tua tatna thu hoih lamdang,
Mohna damsak na thu;
Honhilh hilh in tua tangthu,
Ka mangngilh pahpah hi;
Zingsang daitui thak kia zong,
Sun nisat chiang' mang hi.

Tangthu honhilh, kamdam in,
Chitak deihsak na toh;
Jesu hotdam ding mikhial
Kei hi'ng thei gige in;
Tangthu honhilh gige in,
Mangbatna ka tuah chiang,
Kei ding a hong lungmuanpa
Nong hihnop taktak leh.

Tangthu Kumlui honhilh in,
Leitung thupinate'n
Kei hon susia ding chi a
Non lauhpih peuhpeuh chiang;
He tua leitung thupina'n,
Ka kha hongkhem chiang in,
Tangthu Kumlui honhilh in,
'Jesu'n hondamsak', chi'n.

Lungkhamna mialin hontuam zong,
A chitna hoihna kiam lou;
Miallak pan A vakna tangkhia,
Pathian, itna leh vak hi.

Lungkham mangbat i chihte'n zong,
A hehpihna kilangsak;
I Pathian dangtuan thei ngeilou,
Pathian itna leh vak hi.

476 Vaihawmna Ni Thupi

Doh is G

Vaihawmna ni thupi hongtun in,
Ja ing pengkul a hong ging hi,
Namchih leh chichih hong pungkhawm in,
Ka mu mangtutphah ngou maiah,
Van Angel siangthou a hongkumsuk a,
Tuipi leh leitung tengteng tung ah,
A khut van lam a liktou kawm in ah,
Hun leh ni atawpta a hongchi.

    Ngaidih, kah leh lungkham kikou aw'n,
    Mangthangten atan uh theiin,
    Tang leh mualte kiang ah, hondelh un,
    A thumna uh akai lawta.

Mi sumhaute zong tel sam uh a,
A sum uh tuimang khinta a,
Khutdoh bang maiin Toupa maiah,
A leiba uh din zoulou uh,
Lei mi thupite zong om sam uh a,
Sihna natna thuak in mau uh a,
Angel min gelhna Vanlaibu tawiten
A thupina tuam uh mulou uh.

Meithai leh tagahte zong om uh,
Toupa'n a thumna uh ngaikhia;
Khutdoh lungkham om nawn louhna ah,
A khitui uh a nulsiang ding;
Sum kikap hatte leh zukham hatte,
A kiang ua zu dawnding zuakte toh,
A kiang ua zu zuak phalna petu toh
Gawtmun ah a lut khawmta diam uh.

Hoih kisa a kideihhunte zong
Om uh, ahoihna uh chinglou,
Tang a Jesu kilhlumtute zong,
Mihing ngaih in hoih in lang uh,
Hotdamna simmoh a tu lungmuangte,
Tuin hun omlou awl awl in ah,
Hotdam ka hithouna ding chi tute,
A kikhel sih nihna tangta uh.

477 A Hongtung Ta Khristmas

Doh is Ab

Kum sulhei a hongtun chiangin,
Lungzuan thelbang thousak,
Ngailou leh kipaklou kuamah omlou;
I ngaklah Khristmas ni tuang a hongtung nawn ta,
A etlawm sem din Bethlehem pak toh;
Hongpak lunta e pakbang lawm ni.

    Aw etlawm sang e, hiai nunnop ni hun tomkal sung,
    Vangnei kisa'ng e, nopna ni tuang hongtungta,
    Lung kituak in nunnop zaila'n awi ni,
    Na lungkhamna silhpuan bang paiin.

Omlaivei leh lusunta ten,
Tantawk gel sam dih ua,
Hun mualliamsa teng ngaiin i mau hi;
Pak bang i lopsa hiai ni thupi hongtun chiang,
Sungkuan kim a i lenlai ngaisem hang;
Naubang kahna luankhi tui a luang.

Tung Thianmang hambang honhuai hen,
Nunnuam in zaisa ni,
I lailung sung natna teng damta hen;
I ngaklah ni kipahhuai tuang hongtung nawnta,
Na puakgik tengtengte paikhia inla;
Nunnuam ni hun hoih i neih sung in.

478 Aw Nazareth Jesu

Doh is D

Nazareth Jesu koia pai ding na hi hiam?

Sual tate na itna vangin khros po kawm in,

    Melmate'n pi jel uh, gamdai dam lam zuan in,
    Aw, Nazareth Jesu koia pai ding na hiam?

A hon it ziakin maw, en in mualkhum dekta,
Kapin ka mau jel a, hizong tawp vual a hilou hi.

Nazareth Jesu koia pai ding na hi hiam?
Mipi pungkhawmtein na tungah khros honnga uh,
Hizong Toupa Jesu kei din damna na hi,
Na gam na tun chiangin hon theigige in ka Toupa.

I tangtawn van khopi kongkhak Kalvari i awi ding.

Houlungtuak tangbang dam nunnuam ngabang leng din;
Tungthianmang vanglian in lumbang honsung zel hen,
Itna tongchiam simthu hualkhau khihkip den hen.

Tanglai Kana khua a na tel bangin Toupa,
Taksap teng hongguan din hongngai ung hongleng in;
Lungkham dah leh taksap hun hongtung zel mahleh,
Hiai kitenna siangthou pahtawiin omzel hen.

@ Labu 2019

496 Hon Pahtawi Ung

Rev Thangminlun Mangte
Doh is D

Sianmang simthu lelsa, nihgel anbang ki it,
Tuibang kigawmna ni tuang hongtungta a,
Nuamin honpahtawi ung hiai kitenna siangthou,
Sian in lumbang sung in vualzawl ta hen.

    Nunin nuamin zaila'n pakni Sianmang muanga,
    Damtui bang kigawmte damsung khenlou dinga,
    Khristian innkuan bawl di'n tu leh ta phungching di'n
    Sian in huai hen.

Sanggam aw tuni in, na thilhoih muh lianu,
Na chiin na tuai teng leh Khrist a na unaute'n,
Nuam in honpahtawi ung, hizong Sianmang muang a
Na simthu chiamsa uh khuambang kip hen.

Asiamtu minthanna, innkuan phungching hiding,
Mi siangthou tampite tun leh zua hiding in,
Sian in hongsung henla, siangthou kitenna in,
Asiampa Pasian minthangsak hen.

@ Labu 2019

496A Nang A Hongpai, Aw Hondampa

F R Havergal
Doh is C

Nang na hongpai aw Hondampa!
Nang na hongpai, Kumpipa!
Leichih in na min lou tading,
Nuamsa in lasa ta n'ung!
Nang na hongpai! Zung thupi te'n
Na sih in puanjak keksak;
Khualzinna lampi nuamsakta,
Thupina Nang apan sawl.

    Nang na hongpai! Nang na hongpai!
    Na lampi ah hontuak n'ung!
    Nang na hongpai! Kon mu ding uh.
    Tuani chianga Nang bang ding;
    Nang na hongpai! Nang na hongpai!
    Jesu ka Toupa it uh!
    Aw vaihawmna Nang honmuh ding,
    Biakpen, Pahtawi pen, Itpen.

Nang na hongpai! liap a omlou,
Mei kailou, khitui luanglou;
Khelhna omlou, dahna omlou;
Nisuak thupi leh vakin,
Nang na hongpai! Jesu Hondam,
Bangdang ngaihtuah tham omlou;
Thupi leh nopna lamdang hi,
Tua Na thuakna'n hon leisak.

@ Labu 2019

497 Toupa Phat Un

D Zechech
Doh is Bb

Ka Jesu Ka honpa, nangbang kuadang omlou,
Ka nuntak sung Nang kong phat ding,
Na itna lamdang luat manin
Ka muanna ka tenna ka bitna leh ka hatna
Ka hinsung teng ka pumpi in,
Nangmah biakna tawplou ding.

    Toupa phat un leitung tengteng'n la sa'n
    A vangletna leh lalnate phat in
    Tuipi mau ding tangte kun ding uh,
    Na min a zak hun chiang un,
    Na khutsuakte kipahpi'n la ka sa
    Tangtawn in kon it ding tangtawn a kip di'n,
    Na thuchiam ka neih bangbang tehvual hilou hi.

@ Labu 2019

498 Kulhpi Nahi

V Siampu
Doh is G

Toupa aw kong ngen hi nakhutin honlenin
Na itna hoihna muthei gige di'n
Simlei lungngaihna leh dahna natna lakah,
Nanga muanna kha'n hong dimsak zelin

    Nanglouin muanna omlou,
    Nanglouin damna omlou
    Nanglouin ngaihdamna omlou
    Muanna suangpi nahi, tangtawn hinna nahi,
    Khamuanna nanga om mite hampha

Simlei miza laiah, muanna pethei omlou
Sum leh pai Pilna Siamna haute zong,
Lunglen Lungmuang theilou simlei thawmhau den ah
Khamuanna nanga om mite hampha

Chitna khatzong neilou, hoihna khatzong neilou
Na itna lian in sang hi Toupa aw,
Man ngenlou a hinna hongpia Pathian hoih aw,
Nuamlua ing natungah lungdam lua ing.

@ Labu 2019

499 Jesu, Nang Vang In

Lun Thawmte
Doh is G

Ka Toupa hon itna lamdang lua sa'ng,
Mikhial kei hon itna thukin sang hi;
Khelh vanga siding kei honit manin;
Sing khros tungah sihna hial kei di'n hongtel.

    Mellawm lou tua khros ah kikilhdenpa,
    Aw kei di'n sakmel etlawm pen ahi;
    Gim gentheih zatam thuakin N'ong lei maw!
    Tangtawn hinna neita'ng Jesu, Nang vangin.

Engbawlna linglukhu hon khusak uh,
Mihingte nuihsan leh pampaih in om;
Tuabang teng Na thuak zong sul heilou lai;
Kei vangin maw Toupa hiai bangteng N'ong thuak.

Kalvari tang lam manoh in apai,
A khros puak giksain tawl in apuk;
Bah leh chau in aw kei din apai zel;
A thuakgimna kei di'n lungmuanna ahi.

Khros tungah enghouna chiteng Na thuak,
Simmoh leh bawl gentheih in Na om a;
Na taksa pan sisan hong luangkhia hi;
Tua sisan luang te'n ka khelhna sawp siangta.
Halleluiah Toupa honphat ning e!
Kei dia hinna lampi N'ong bawlsak vang'n
Ka moh N'ong maisakta ka batteng zong,
Tun kei suakta hi ta'ng Jesu Nang vang in.

@ Labu 2019

500 Hinna Hongpia

T Pumkhothang
Doh is Gb M72

Hinna hongpia ka Toupa hong it ing,
Mangthang lungngai ka vaih laiin,
Lunglaigil ah khamuanna Nong pia,
Muanna tuibang na hong luanna.

    Hinna hongpia ka Toupa aw,
    Nanglou muanna ding ka nei ngei diam?
    Lungngai huibang ka mauna simlei ah,
    Nang toh omleng ka lung nuam hi.

Suan ding omlou ka hoihna zong omlou,
Nang toh om di'n ka ching zoulou,
Hizong Toupa na itna aw nem toh,
Kong it chiin Na hong samlai.

Keimah lampi ka zuih khempeuhte leh,
Ka lunggel leh ka ngaihtuahna,
Toupa nang di'n a chingzou ding omlou,
Hizong kong it ka ta nong chi.

@ Labu 2019

500A Khawlni Toupa

P Doddridge
Doh is Bb

Khawlni Toupa, thumna ngai in,
Na inn ah hongleng ung, Nang Ni'n,
Nang biakna thu genin, la sa'n,
Gimnamtui bang hong jamtou hen.

Simlei khawlni nonpiak bawn nuam,
Ka laukha semgim leh liangvai;
A tutkhawl kumkhuana ding ah,
Vana khawlni na bawl ngakla'ng.

Thangvan khawlni a hongtun chia'n,
Dahna leh thumnate tengteng,
Kipahna mun ka tun chiangin,
Tuate van ah om nawnlou ding.

Dougal laang laang nawnta lou ding,
Nunnop tutkhawl sunni bei toh,
Sunnitum a, muikhua zing lou,
Vanglian Toupa sunni bang tang.

Lunggulh kumsawt khawlni kipan,
Toupa leh Amah mi te toh,
Nunkhua nuam in, tawp ngeikei ni,
Nunnop zaila sa'n kumvei ni.

@ Labu 2019
